< Text>
Experience was great. I sat at the sushi bar and was greeted by the server and the sushi chef. I ended up there between 5 and 5:15. They had a happy hour so I got the sabe tequila which reminded me of Clase Azul Blanco premium Tequila.
The Hildebrand roll was really good. It's just hard to eat because it was so big. I ended up eating the tops then the rolls. The soft shell crab is battered in their house, scratch made, tempura batter. Super crispy!!! Made me think of freshly refried cornflakes or potato chips, gave the roll a nice crunch.

The Miso soup was nice, it had shredded nori and a good amount of green onion on/in it.

The Mango icecream seemed yogurt based to me. The flavor was good but I personally prefer less yogurt flavor.  I look forward to trying the black sesame ice cream.

I look forward to trying the sushi/sashimi plates.

Just wish they had more specialty gluten free options for rolls and I will plan to bring my tamari from home. Luckily, I had my gluten enzyme tablets with me.< /Text>

< review>
Fast, easy, and cheap.

Solid burger and fries at a really good value. I like the quarter ponder with cheese and fries combo. These are good old fashion burgers with nothing crazy going on like a lot of the new spots.

They have a lot of other options besides burgers and offer breakfast.

If you are trying to get a decent meal on a budget, come by. If you are looking for gourmet burgers, probably look elsewhere.

On a side note, this is one of my go to spots after a night of drinking. Nothing like a burger and fries to make it all better.< /review>

<Review>So far, I've only been here for a few community meetings.  From what I've seen, everything is excellent.  The place is very clean, new and well-maintained, including the bathrooms.  The big community room is huge and they have a smaller meeting room too.  Free parking is ample.  There are tennis and volleyball courts.  And spacious playground areas with equipment for kids.  They set up the Fallbrook Christmas tree right outside.  Inexpensive lunches for seniors are provided every week day.  There are other programs relating to health and culture.  Not sure what else to say except it seems to be everything a community center should be.</Review>< username>

Brass tacks; the food was pretty good, not fantastic. We ordered 7 unique meals, plus appetizers to get a full spectrum, and the street noodles were very tasty as was the steak. <userid>100690361339193183043< /userid><username>T J<//username><Time>1468804705862</Time><Rating>3<//Rating>< text>
Had dinner at P.F. Chang's in Roseville for the first time. There were several reviews about the wait for food but we figured it was just a one off situation... nope it wasn't. We waited 10 minutes for a table but we had a reservation while other were waiting for 30 minutes.

We were seated and it took 10 minutes to order drinks and 10 more to get them. Once we had our drinks we order appetizers that took 30 minutes. 10 minutes after we ordered apps, we order our dinner. It took them another 30 minutes after our appetizers were served for the dinner to come out. From the time we were seated, it was an hour and 20 minutes for our dinner.

The edemame had very little sea salt which made them bland. The lobster roll was bland until I added some wasabi. The dinners were lacking flavor also. I'm not sure if you have been to Pei Wei but it is like P.F. Chang's and cheaper. Pei Wei flavor are more robust so I was expecting P.F. Chang's to be comparable or better, it wasn't.

Our server was very nice but apparently dealing with a complaint at another table so getting our check took another 20 minutes after we were done. The waiter thanked us for our patience, almost as if it was the norm.<//text>
